-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `holescores`
--

CREATE TABLE `holescores` (
  `id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `score` int(10) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `hole_id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `round_id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `updated_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `holescores_score_index` (`score`),
  KEY `holescores_hole_id_index` (`hole_id`),
  KEY `holescores_round_id_index` (`round_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci AUTO_INCREMENT=3655 ;

--
-- Table structure for table `skins`
--

CREATE TABLE `skins` (
  `id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `player_id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `level_id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `match_id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `hole_id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `money` decimal(12,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `updated_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `skins_player_id_index` (`player_id`),
  KEY `skins_level_id_index` (`level_id`),
  KEY `skins_match_id_index` (`match_id`),
  KEY `skins_hole_id_index` (`hole_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci AUTO_INCREMENT=202 ;

--
-- Table structure for table `users`
--

CREATE TABLE `users` (
  `id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `username` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `password` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `confirmation_code` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `remember_token` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `confirmed` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `updated_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `users_username_unique` (`username`),
  UNIQUE KEY `users_email_unique` (`email`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci AUTO_INCREMENT=2 ;

--
-- Table structure for table `winners`
--

CREATE TABLE `winners` (
  `id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `player_id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `game_id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `match_id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `updated_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `winners_player_id_index` (`player_id`),
  KEY `winners_game_id_index` (`game_id`),
  KEY `winners_match_id_index` (`match_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;
